\makeatletter\def\@hexadecimal#1{\ifcase#1\or 0\or 1\or 2\or 3\or 4\or 5\or 6\or 7\or 8\or 9\or A\or B\or C\or D\or E\or F\else\@ctrerr\fi\relax}
\def\hexadecimal#1{\expandafter\@hexadecimal\csname c@#1\endcsname}
\renewcommand\thesection{\bfseries\hexadecimal{section}\#\#\#\#}
\renewcommand\thesubsection{\bfseries\hexadecimal{section}\hexadecimal{subsection}\#\#\#}
\renewcommand\thesubsubsection{\bfseries\hexadecimal{section}\hexadecimal{subsection}\hexadecimal{subsubsection}\#\#}
